### 1. Immigration, Refugees and Citizenship Canada - Canada.ca

- **重要性:** 1.00

It offers resources for checking application statuses, applying for visas and permits, and accessing support for settling in Canada. Additionally, the site includes alerts regarding special measures for specific countries and highlights key services for both potential immigrants and Canadian citizens.

### 6. Atlantic Immigration Program - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/services/immigrate-canada/atlantic-immigration.html
- **重要性:** 1.00
- **深度:** 5
- **链接数:** 59
- **摘要:** The Atlantic Immigration Program offers a pathway to permanent residence for skilled foreign workers and international graduates from Canadian institutions who wish to live and work in one of Canada’s four Atlantic provinces: New Brunswick, Nova Scotia, Prince Edward Island, or Newfoundland and Labrador. To participate, candidates must secure a job offer from a designated employer in the region, and employers must first become designated by their provincial government. The program aims to fill labor shortages in these provinces by facilitating the hiring of qualified international candidates.

### 7. Work permit: How to apply - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/services/work-canada/permit/temporary/apply.html
- **重要性:** 1.00
- **深度:** 9
- **链接数:** 85
- **摘要:** The Canada.ca webpage on applying for a work permit outlines the updated application process, stating that most foreign nationals in Canada can no longer apply at a port of entry and must now apply online for both initial permits and extensions. Those outside Canada may still apply upon arrival at a port of entry, while priority processing is available for certain essential service occupations. The page emphasizes the importance of having the necessary documents and reading the instruction guide before submitting an application online.

### 10. Work in Canada after you graduate: About the post-graduation work permit (PGWP) - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/services/study-canada/work/after-graduation/about.html
- **重要性:** 1.00
- **深度:** 10
- **链接数:** 72
- **摘要:** The post-graduation work permit (PGWP) allows international students who have graduated from eligible Canadian institutions to work in Canada and gain valuable experience. Eligibility for the PGWP is not automatic upon graduation, and as of November 1, 2024, new requirements have been introduced, although certain applicants may be exempt. The duration of the PGWP depends on the length of the study program and the validity of the applicant's passport.

### 11. Extend or change the conditions on your work permit: How to apply - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/services/work-canada/permit/temporary/extend/apply.html

- **深度:** 10
- **链接数:** 91
- **摘要:** The Canada.ca webpage provides essential information on how to extend or change the conditions of a work permit in Canada. Applicants must submit their application before their current permit expires to maintain legal status during processing; this can be done either online or via paper. The page also highlights the importance of obtaining a positive Labour Market Impact Assessment (LMIA) from the employer for certain jobs before applying for a work permit.

### 12. How to check your application status - Canada.ca

Applicants can select their specific application type (e.g., adult, minor, Canadian Armed Forces member) and are informed about the importance of receiving an acknowledgment of receipt (AOR) letter or email after submitting their application. The page emphasizes that processing times can vary and encourages users to confirm their application status through the appropriate channels.

Key requirements include demonstrating intent to leave Canada upon expiration of the permit, financial stability, good health, and lack of criminal records. The page also specifies different criteria for applicants applying from outside or inside Canada, including specific conditions related to valid permits and the potential for expedited processing through the Global Skills Strategy.

There are two main types of permits: employer-specific and open work permits. Additionally, the page outlines options for bringing family members who may also be allowed to work or study in Canada, along with details on fees starting at $155 and variable processing times depending on the applicant's country.

### 15. Immigrate through the Atlantic Immigration Program: Apply for permanent residence - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/services/immigrate-canada/atlantic-immigration/how-to-immigrate/permanent-residence.html
- **重要性:** 1.00
- **深度:** 10
- **链接数:** 98
- **摘要:** The Atlantic Immigration Program enables individuals to apply for permanent residence in Canada, with a mandatory online application process introduced on October 21, 2022. Applicants must provide biometrics and complete various digital and PDF forms, including the Generic Application Form and additional family information. A detailed Instruction Guide and Document Checklist are available to assist applicants in ensuring they meet eligibility requirements and submit all necessary documents.

### 16. Immigrate through the Atlantic Immigration Program: Who can apply - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/services/immigrate-canada/atlantic-immigration/how-to-immigrate/eligibility.html
- **重要性:** 1.00
- **深度:** 10
- **链接数:** 83
- **摘要:** The Atlantic Immigration Program in Canada allows individuals to apply for immigration if they meet specific eligibility criteria, including having qualifying work experience, educational qualifications, and language proficiency. Applicants must demonstrate sufficient financial resources and, if already living in Canada on a valid work permit, do not need to provide proof of funds. The program emphasizes the importance of recent work experience, requiring at least 1,560 hours of paid work in the last five years, and encourages candidates to seek employment with designated Atlantic employers.

### 17. Immigrate through the Atlantic Immigration Program - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/services/immigrate-canada/atlantic-immigration/how-to-immigrate.html
- **重要性:** 1.00
- **深度:** 10
- **链接数:** 63
- **摘要:** The Atlantic Immigration Program (AIP) is a Canadian immigration pathway aimed at skilled foreign workers and international graduates who wish to live and work in one of the four Atlantic provinces. This employer-driven initiative requires candidates to secure a job offer from a designated employer in Atlantic Canada, and applicants can be either recent graduates from local post-secondary institutions or skilled workers. The program facilitates the hiring of qualified candidates for positions that local employers are unable to fill.

The guide outlines eligibility criteria, application procedures (primarily online), and necessary steps, such as submitting biometrics. It emphasizes that while most applications must be submitted online, exceptions exist for certain situations, including disabilities or technical issues with the online system.

### 19. Sponsor your spouse, partner or child: Optional: Open work permit in Canada - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/services/immigrate-canada/family-sponsorship/spouse-partner-children/spouse-common-law-partner-canada-open-work-permit.html
- **重要性:** 1.00
- **深度:** 10
- **链接数:** 84
- **摘要:** This webpage provides information on how spouses, common-law partners, or dependent children of permanent residents in Canada can apply for an open work permit while their permanent residence application is being processed. To be eligible, applicants must be in a genuine relationship with their sponsor, reside in Canada with them, and have received an acknowledgment of receipt (AOR) letter for their permanent residence application. The page also notes that accompanying dependent children must meet specific requirements related to their principal applicant's status and living arrangements.

### 23. Extend your study permit or restore your status: How to apply - Canada.ca

- **摘要:** The Canada.ca webpage provides essential information on how to extend a study permit or restore status for international students in Canada. It highlights that most applicants already in Canada cannot apply for a study permit at a port of entry and must do so online, while those applying from outside Canada may still do so upon arrival. Key requirements include obtaining a letter of acceptance or enrolment from a designated learning institution (DLI) and ensuring that the DLI validates this letter within the specified timeframe to avoid application delays.

These conditions include being enrolled in a designated learning institution, actively pursuing studies, and applying for an extension or changing schools as needed. Additionally, the page notes that study permit holders may have specific conditions related to their level of studies, work permissions, and other requirements that must be followed to avoid losing their permit or student status.

### 25. Study permit: How to apply - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/services/study-canada/study-permit/apply.html
- **重要性:** 1.00
- **深度:** 9
- **链接数:** 111
- **摘要:** To apply for a study permit in Canada, you generally need to do so before arriving, although some exceptions allow applications from within Canada or at the port of entry. Key requirements include a letter of acceptance from a designated learning institution and a provincial or territorial attestation letter, which must be submitted with your application. Applications must be completed online, with specific provisions for certain individuals who cannot apply online due to disabilities or other circumstances.

### 26. Study permit: Who can apply - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/services/study-canada/study-permit/eligibility.html
- **重要性:** 1.00
- **深度:** 10
- **链接数:** 77
- **摘要:** The webpage provides information on the eligibility requirements for international students applying for a study permit in Canada. To qualify, applicants must be enrolled in a designated learning institution (DLI), demonstrate sufficient financial resources, maintain good health, and have no criminal record. Additionally, the page outlines the responsibilities of students while studying and mentions the possibility of obtaining a post-graduation work permit (PGWP) after completing their studies, highlighting the importance of checking program eligibility.

### 27. Study permit - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/services/study-canada/study-permit.html
- **重要性:** 1.00
- **深度:** 10
- **链接数:** 63
- **摘要:** To apply for a study permit in Canada, international students need to obtain a provincial attestation letter (PAL) or territorial attestation letter (TAL) from the relevant province or territory, as most applications submitted without these will be returned. The study permit, which costs CAD 150, is essential for studying at designated learning institutions (DLIs) in Canada, and applicants are advised to gather all necessary documents before applying. Processing times for study permits vary by country, and it's important to ensure that any immigration representatives are authorized to assist with the application.

Applicants are advised to submit their application at least 30 days before their current status expires, with specific guidelines on determining the expiry date based on their entry documentation.

- **摘要:** The webpage on Canada.ca provides guidance on whether individuals need a study permit to study in Canada, depending on the duration and nature of their study program. It outlines various scenarios, indicating that students studying for six months or less typically do not require a permit, while others, including those in Quebec or specific circumstances like family members of foreign representatives, may have different requirements. Additionally, the page explains that a study permit is not a visa but can include authorization to enter Canada upon approval.

### 32. Extend your study permit or restore your status: When to apply - Canada.ca

- **深度:** 7
- **链接数:** 66
- **摘要:** The Canadian government provides guidelines for extending study permits or restoring status for international students. Applications to extend a study permit must be submitted at least 30 days before the current permit expires, and students can remain in Canada under the same conditions while awaiting a decision if they apply on time. Key factors affecting the expiration of a study permit include early or late completion of studies and changes in the status of the educational institution.

### 34. Study permit: Get the right documents - Canada.ca

- **重要性:** 1.00

- **链接数:** 83
- **摘要:** To apply for a study permit in Canada, you must provide several key documents, including proof of acceptance from an educational institution, a provincial or territorial attestation letter, proof of identity, and proof of financial support. Additional documents may be required depending on your circumstances, such as a letter of explanation, a medical exam, or a custodian declaration for minors. This information is essential for international students seeking to study in Canada.

### 42. Designated learning institutions in Canada - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/services/study-canada/educational-institutions.html
- **重要性:** 1.00

### 59. Valid passports and other travel documents needed to come to Canada - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/services/passport-travel-document.html
- **重要性:** 1.00
- **深度:** 10
- **链接数:** 56
- **摘要:** To travel to Canada, you must possess a valid passport or travel document that is legal, not expired, and accepted by Immigration, Refugees and Citizenship Canada (IRCC). If applying for permits or permanent residency, ensure your passport is valid for at least six months and has at least one free page for visa stamps. Certain documents, such as passports from Somalia and non-machine readable passports from the Czech Republic, are deemed unreliable and not accepted for travel to Canada.

### 79. What is a temporary resident visa (TRV)? - Canada.ca

- **摘要:** The "Temporary workers: Eligibility and admissibility" section on Canada.ca provides detailed guidelines and policies for the Temporary Foreign Workers Program and the International Mobility Program, outlining the necessary steps to assess work permit applications. ### 83. Who must submit to an immigration medical exam (IME) - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/corporate/publications-manuals/operational-bulletins-manuals/standard-requirements/medical-requirements/exam/who-must-submit-immigration-medical-examination.html
- **重要性:** 1.00
- **深度:** 9
- **链接数:** 83
- **摘要:** Foreign nationals applying for permanent residence in Canada, along with their family members, are required to undergo an immigration medical examination (IME) to ensure they do not pose a risk to public health or safety and do not place excessive demand on health services. A valid medical certificate must be obtained before a final decision on their application can be made. Non-accompanying family members only need to complete one IME and are not required to repeat the exam if it has expired, although reassessment may be necessary for processing.

It serves as a resource for stakeholders and provides guidance for the IRCC staff involved in the immigration process.

### 101. Super visa for parents and grandparents: What is a super visa - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/services/visit-canada/parent-grandparent-super-visa/about.html
- **重要性:** 1.00
- **深度:** 8
- **链接数:** 68
- **摘要:** The Super Visa allows parents and grandparents of Canadian citizens or permanent residents to visit Canada for up to 5 years at a time, with multiple entries permitted over a 10-year period. Applicants must meet specific requirements, including obtaining health insurance, and must ensure their passport remains valid during their stay. For shorter visits of 6 months or less, a standard visitor visa is recommended.

### 103. Biometrics Where to give your fingerprints and photo - Canada.ca

- **摘要:** The Canada.ca webpage provides essential information about where and how to give biometrics (fingerprints and photos) for Canadian immigration purposes. Applicants must book free appointments within 30 days of receiving their biometric instruction letter (BIL) and can do so at various visa application centers (VACs) around the world. If unable to provide biometrics within the timeframe, applicants are advised to inform IRCC of their intended biometric collection location, which can be either inside or outside Canada.

### 108. Apply for citizenship: How to apply - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/services/canadian-citizenship/become-canadian-citizen/apply.html

- **摘要:** The webpage provides detailed information on how to apply for Canadian citizenship, highlighting the options for online and paper applications. Applicants are advised to choose one application method and ensure all required documents are included with their submission.

### 109. Apply for citizenship: Who can apply - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/services/canadian-citizenship/become-canadian-citizen/eligibility.html
- **重要性:** 1.00
- **深度:** 10
- **链接数:** 100
- **摘要:** To apply for Canadian citizenship, you must be a permanent resident who has lived in Canada for at least three of the last five years, filed taxes if required, demonstrated language proficiency, passed a citizenship test, and taken the oath of citizenship. There are specific eligibility criteria for different groups, including minors, spouses of Canadian citizens, and former citizens seeking to regain their citizenship. It's important to check your eligibility based on your situation, as certain conditions may prevent you from obtaining citizenship.

### 110. Apply for Canadian citizenship - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/services/canadian-citizenship/become-canadian-citizen.html
- **重要性:** 1.00
- **深度:** 10
- **链接数:** 56
- **摘要:** To apply for Canadian citizenship, applicants must be permanent residents, have lived in Canada for at least three out of the last five years, file taxes if required, pass a citizenship test, demonstrate language proficiency in English or French, and take the citizenship oath. Applications can be submitted online or on paper, with fees set at $649.75 for adults and $100 for minors, although the adult fee will increase to $119.75 on March 31, 2025. After applying, applicants will receive a confirmation letter if their application is complete, and they can access various resources for new citizens upon approval.

### 147. If your Express Entry application is approved - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/services/immigrate-canada/express-entry/application-approved.html
- **重要性:** 1.00
- **深度:** 10
- **链接数:** 73
- **摘要:** If your Express Entry application is approved by the Government of Canada, you will receive a Confirmation of Permanent Residence (COPR) and, if applicable, a permanent resident visa. It's crucial to verify that the information on your COPR matches your passport, as errors must be corrected promptly. You must travel to Canada before your COPR expires and present it to border services upon arrival, or use it for applying for government services if you are already in Canada.

### 149. Immigrate through Express Entry - Canada.ca

### 150. Express Entry: Federal Skilled Trades Program - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/services/immigrate-canada/express-entry/eligibility/skilled-trades.html
- **重要性:** 1.00
- **深度:** 9
- **链接数:** 110
- **摘要:** The Federal Skilled Trades Program allows skilled workers in specific trades to apply for permanent residency in Canada. Eligible applicants must demonstrate relevant work experience in designated skilled trade sectors, possess a valid job offer or certificate of qualification, and meet language proficiency and education requirements. Key sectors include construction, transportation, manufacturing, and natural resources, with candidates needing at least two years of paid work experience within the past five years.

### 151. Express Entry: Federal Skilled Worker Program - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/services/immigrate-canada/express-entry/eligibility/federal-skilled-workers.html
- **重要性:** 1.00
- **深度:** 9
- **链接数:** 101
- **摘要:** The Federal Skilled Worker Program under Canada's Express Entry system is designed for skilled workers with foreign work experience seeking permanent residency. Applicants must meet specific criteria, including having relevant skilled work experience categorized under TEER 0, 1, 2, or 3, and must demonstrate proficiency in areas such as education, language skills, and job duties as outlined in the National Occupational Classification (NOC). To be eligible, candidates must provide proof of their skilled work experience, which must be paid and acquired within the last ten years, totaling at least one year of continuous work or 1,560 hours.

### 159. Immigrate through the Economic Mobility Pathways Pilot: How the pilot works - Canada.ca

### 160. Immigrate through the Economic Mobility Pathways Pilot: Who can apply - Canada.ca

- **链接数:** 74
- **摘要:** The Economic Mobility Pathways Pilot (EMPP) allows refugees and displaced persons to immigrate to Canada by meeting specific eligibility requirements. Applicants must provide proof of their refugee status, such as a positive Refugee Status Determination or registration with the UN Refugee Agency, and must be residing outside Canada at the time of application. They can apply based on their work experience, education, and language skills, or through an economic immigration program, with potential access to loans for settlement funds.

### 173. Provincial Nominee Program : Express Entry process Who can apply - Canada.ca

Applicants must be nominated by a province and qualify for one of the three Express Entry programs: the Federal Skilled Worker Program, the Federal Skilled Trades Program, or the Canadian Experience Class. Each province has its own PNP streams, and interested candidates should review the respective province's website for detailed eligibility requirements and nomination processes.

### 174. Interim Federal Health Program: What is covered - Canada.ca

- **深度:** 7
- **链接数:** 65
- **摘要:** The Interim Federal Health Program (IFHP) in Canada provides temporary health care coverage for specific groups, including resettled refugees and refugee claimants, who are not eligible for provincial or territorial health insurance. The program covers essential medical services such as hospital care, physician services, vaccinations, and pre-departure medical necessities for refugees. However, it does not cover costs that are claimable under other insurance plans and does not coordinate benefits with other programs.

### 178. Claiming refugee protection (asylum) at the border when you enter Canada - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/services/asylum/border.html
- **重要性:** 1.00
- **深度:** 6
- **链接数:** 63
- **摘要:** Canada provides refugee protection to individuals who have a well-founded fear of persecution or face risks such as torture or life-threatening situations if returned to their home country. Those seeking asylum at a Canadian port of entry must demonstrate these risks; the process differs for claims made from within the country. It is important to apply for refugee protection only if genuinely at risk, as false claims may lead to removal and a ban on returning to Canada.

### 179. Meet the requirements to submit a refugee claim - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/services/asylum/border/eligibility.html
- **重要性:** 1.00
- **深度:** 7
- **链接数:** 64
- **摘要:** The webpage outlines the eligibility requirements for submitting a refugee claim in Canada, emphasizing that certain conditions may render a claim ineligible, such as being recognized as a Convention refugee in another country or having a previous claim rejected. It also highlights the implications of the Canada-U.S. Safe Third Country Agreement, which affects individuals entering Canada from the U.S. and seeking asylum. If eligibility requirements are met, claims are forwarded to the Immigration and Refugee Board of Canada for determination; otherwise, individuals may face removal from Canada.

### 185. Canada-U.S. Safe Third Country Agreement - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/corporate/mandate/policies-operational-instructions-agreements/agreements/safe-third-country-agreement.html
- **重要性:** 1.00
- **深度:** 8
- **链接数:** 70
- **摘要:** The Canada-U.S. Safe Third Country Agreement (STCA) remains in effect, requiring individuals entering Canada from the U.S. to make refugee claims in the U.S. unless they meet specific exceptions. As of March 25, 2023, the STCA has been expanded to cover the entire land border, including internal waterways, meaning that those who cross to seek asylum will be returned to the U.S. if they do not qualify for an exemption. This agreement is designed to streamline the management of refugee claims between the two countries.

Notably, those wishing to sponsor refugees in Quebec must apply through the provincial government.

### 217. Atlantic Immigration Program - Canada.ca

- **重要性:** 1.00
- **深度:** 9
- **链接数:** 59
- **摘要:** The Atlantic Immigration Program offers a pathway to permanent residence in Canada for skilled foreign workers and international graduates from Canadian institutions who wish to live and work in one of the four Atlantic provinces: New Brunswick, Nova Scotia, Prince Edward Island, or Newfoundland and Labrador. To participate, applicants must secure a job offer from a designated employer in the region, and employers must undergo a designation process to hire qualified international candidates. The program aims to address local labor shortages and supports both job seekers and employers.

### 218. Atlantic Immigration Program: Language testing - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/services/immigrate-canada/atlantic-immigration/language-testing.html
- **重要性:** 1.00
- **深度:** 9
- **链接数:** 86
- **摘要:** The Atlantic Immigration Program requires applicants to prove their language proficiency in English or French through approved tests, such as CELPIP or IELTS for English, and TEF or TCF for French. Test results must be less than two years old, and applicants must achieve minimum scores based on their job's National Occupational Classification (NOC) category, with CLB 5 required for TEER 0-3 jobs and CLB 4 for TEER 4 jobs. Applicants should include a copy of their test results with their application.

### 219. Atlantic Immigration Program: How to get an educational credential assessment - Canada.ca

The ECA must be issued by a designated organization and be less than five years old at the time of application. The webpage lists designated organizations and explains the importance of the ECA in the immigration process for the Atlantic Immigration Program.

### 228. Self-employed person: Selection criteria - Canada.ca

### 238. Educational credential assessment - Canada.ca

- **重要性:** 1.00

- **链接数:** 179
- **摘要:** The webpage from Canada.ca provides essential information about the Educational Credential Assessment (ECA), which is necessary for individuals who have completed their education outside Canada and wish to immigrate through the Express Entry system. ### 239. Permanent resident travel document: About the process - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/services/permanent-residents/travel-document.html?wbdisable=true

- **链接数:** 62
- **摘要:** The webpage from Immigration, Refugees and Citizenship Canada (IRCC) outlines the process for applying for a Permanent Resident Travel Document (PRTD), which is necessary for individuals outside Canada who do not possess a valid Permanent Resident (PR) card. A PRTD allows for a single entry into Canada and is typically required when a PR card is expired, lost, stolen, or damaged. It is advised to apply for a new PR card upon returning to Canada, and the processing of PRTD applications is prioritized, though fees and processing times can vary.

### 246. Temporary Foreign Worker - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/employment-social-development/programs/temporary-foreign-worker.html
- **重要性:** 1.00
- **深度:** 10
- **链接数:** 56
- **摘要:** The Temporary Foreign Worker (TFW) Program in Canada allows employers to hire foreign workers for temporary positions when qualified Canadians are unavailable. This program is regulated under the Immigration and Refugee Protection Act and is administered by Employment and Social Development Canada (ESDC) in collaboration with Immigration, Refugees and Citizenship Canada (IRCC) and the Canada Border Services Agency (CBSA). ESDC assesses employer applications and conducts Labour Market Impact Assessments to evaluate the potential effects on the Canadian labor market while ensuring compliance and program integrity.

It outlines the guidelines for identifying and supporting refugees, as well as the process for making asylum claims in Canada, including eligibility determinations at entry points and inland offices. This resource is aimed at stakeholders and individuals seeking to understand the operational framework for refugee protection in Canada.

### 282. Apply for Canadian citizenship - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/services/canadian-citizenship/become-canadian-citizen/about.html
- **重要性:** 1.00
- **深度:** 10
- **链接数:** 56
- **摘要:** To apply for Canadian citizenship, applicants must be permanent residents, have lived in Canada for at least 1,095 days over the last five years, file taxes if required, pass a citizenship test, prove language skills in English or French, and take the citizenship oath. Applications can be submitted online or via paper, with fees set at $649.75 for adults and $100 for minors; note that the adult fee will increase to $119.75 in March 2025. After submission, the application undergoes processing that includes a test, interview, and ceremony, with information available for new citizens on various services.

Resources for studying and what to do if you miss the test are also included.

### 292. Immigration options for victims of family violence - Canada.ca

- **链接数:** 90
- **摘要:** The webpage outlines immigration options for victims of family violence in Canada, specifically highlighting the temporary resident permit (TRP) available to those in abusive situations. As of February 4, 2025, victims can obtain a TRP for at least 12 months without incurring fees for the permit, work permits, study permits, or biometrics. This permit allows victims to remain in Canada safely while considering their next steps, and it can also be extended or issued for accompanying children.

### 296. Rural and Northern Immigration Pilot: Proof of funds - Canada.ca

Recent updates have adjusted the required amounts based on the timing of the community recommendation application.

### 331. Application for Canadian Citizenship: Minors – Subsection 5(1) - Canada.ca

- **摘要:** The webpage provides information on the application process for Canadian citizenship for minors under subsection 5(1). ### 336. Francophone Community Immigration Pilots: Who can apply - Canada.ca

In 2024, the IRCC finalized more than 7 million decisions across various immigration programs, indicating ongoing efforts to improve efficiency and capacity.

The application process can be completed online or by mail, and applicants must ensure they meet eligibility requirements before applying.

### 357. How to sponsor a refugee - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/services/refugees/help-outside-canada/private-sponsorship-program.html
- **重要性:** 0.90

- **摘要:** The Canadian government allows citizens and organizations to sponsor refugees from abroad to resettle in Canada. Sponsorship typically lasts one year and requires financial support for the refugees, as well as assistance in finding employment and integrating into the community. Interested sponsors must be part of a recognized group, such as a sponsorship agreement holder, a group of five, or a community sponsor, and those wishing to sponsor refugees specifically for Quebec must apply through the provincial government.

### 359. Government-Assisted Refugees program - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/services/refugees/resettle-refugee/government-assisted-refugee-program.html
- **重要性:** 0.90
- **深度:** 7
- **链接数:** 74
- **摘要:** The Government-Assisted Refugees (GAR) program in Canada provides a pathway for refugees referred by the UNHCR or other organizations to resettle in Canada with government support. Refugees do not apply directly; instead, they must register with the UNHCR to be considered for the program. The support includes assistance from service provider organizations for up to one year, or until the individual can support themselves, with a specific stream available for human rights defenders and their families, allowing for the resettlement of up to 250 individuals annually.

Eligible Iranian temporary residents can apply for work permits or study permits, while those seeking to extend their stay as visitors or study permit holders must follow the standard application processes starting March 1, 2025, with applicable fees. Additionally, Canadian citizens and permanent residents in Iran will no longer receive fee exemptions for replacing travel documents or citizenship certificates after this date.

### 394. Who can apply - Canada.ca

There are two streams available: one for workers already in Canada and another for applicants not currently working in Canada, which will open at a later date.

### 395. International Mobility Program – Get to know your rights while working in Canada - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/corporate/publications-manuals/know-your-rights-worker-international-mobility-program.html
- **重要性:** 0.90
- **深度:** 8
- **链接数:** 101
- **摘要:** The International Mobility Program in Canada ensures that temporary foreign workers have the same rights and protections as Canadian citizens and permanent residents. Employers are required to provide essential information about workers' rights, a signed employment agreement, appropriate wages, and a safe workplace free from abuse. Additionally, workers cannot be forced into unsafe working conditions or face retaliation for reporting mistreatment.

### 396. Extend or change the conditions on your work permit: Changing jobs or employers - Canada.ca

- **摘要:** The webpage provides information for individuals holding employer-specific work permits in Canada who wish to change jobs or employers. To do so, they must apply for a new work permit and meet specific eligibility criteria. Additionally, those with open work permits can change employers freely, and there is a process to request work authorization while the new permit application is being processed.

### 397. Immigrate through the Home Care Worker Immigration pilots - Settling in Canada - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/services/immigrate-canada/caregivers/home-care-worker-immigration-pilots/child-care-home-support/settle.html

### 398. Rural and Northern Immigration Pilot Program: Language testing - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/services/immigrate-canada/rural-northern-immigration-pilot/language-testing.html
- **重要性:** 0.90
- **深度:** 10
- **链接数:** 71
- **摘要:** The Rural and Northern Immigration Pilot Program in Canada requires applicants to demonstrate their language proficiency in English or French through approved tests, with minimum Canadian Language Benchmark (CLB) scores varying based on the National Occupational Classification (NOC) category of the job offer. Accepted tests include CELPIP and IELTS, and applicants must submit test results that are less than two years old with their application. The minimum language requirements are CLB 6 for TEER 0 or 1 jobs, CLB 5 for TEER 2 or 3, and CLB 4 for TEER 4 or 5.

### 399. Hire through the Atlantic Immigration Program: Optional: Temporary Work Permit - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/services/immigrate-canada/atlantic-immigration/hire-immigrant/temporary-work-permit.html
- **重要性:** 0.80
- **深度:** 7
- **链接数:** 68
- **摘要:** The Atlantic Immigration Program allows candidates who qualify for permanent residence to apply for a temporary work permit while their application is processed. This employer-specific permit is valid for two years and requires a referral letter from the provincial government during the endorsement application. While international graduates from recognized post-secondary institutions in Atlantic Canada are exempt from work experience requirements, other candidates must demonstrate they meet specific language, education, and work experience criteria.

### 400. Immigrate through the Atlantic Immigration Program: Apply for a temporary work permit (optional) - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/services/immigrate-canada/atlantic-immigration/how-to-immigrate/temporary-work-permit.html

- **链接数:** 271
- **摘要:** The Atlantic Immigration Program allows eligible individuals to apply for a temporary work permit while their permanent residence application is being processed. This work permit, valid for two years, is specific to designated employers in Atlantic Canada and requires a job offer and a referral letter from the province. Applicants must also meet certain language, education, and work experience requirements, and their spouses or common-law partners may apply for an open work permit.

### 415. International students travelling outside Canada and then re-entering - Canada.ca

To do so, they must possess a valid study permit or an approval for a study permit extension, along with a valid passport, and meet other entry requirements, such as having a visitor visa or an electronic travel authorization (eTA). ### 418. Electronic travel authorization (eTA): Citizens from some visa-required countries - Canada.ca

### 419. Electronic travel authorization (eTA): Who can apply - Canada.ca

- **摘要:** The webpage provides information on the Electronic Travel Authorization (eTA) required for certain travelers to Canada. Visa-exempt foreign nationals must obtain an eTA if flying to or transiting through a Canadian airport, while U.S. citizens and Canadian permanent residents are exempt from this requirement. Those from visa-required countries need a visitor visa instead of an eTA when traveling by air, but can enter Canada without one when arriving by land or sea.

### 420. Electronic travel authorization (eTA): About the process - Canada.ca

- **摘要:** The webpage provides information about the Electronic Travel Authorization (eTA) required for travelers flying to Canada. The eTA application is a straightforward online process that costs CAD $7 and is typically processed within minutes, although it can take longer in some cases. It is important to note that an eTA does not permit work or study in Canada; separate permits are required for those activities.

### 438. Temporary resident permits: applying for permanent residence - Canada.ca

- **摘要:** The webpage from Canada.ca provides guidance on the eligibility criteria and processes for Temporary Resident Permit (TRP) holders applying for permanent residence in Canada. To qualify, TRP holders must have a valid permit, have resided continuously in Canada for three to five years, and not have become inadmissible for reasons beyond their original TRP. However, any breaks in continuity, such as leaving Canada without authorization or failing to apply for a new permit on time, can disqualify them from permanent residency.

### 451. Open work permits for vulnerable workers [R207.1 – A72] – International Mobility Program (IMP) - Canada.ca

- **摘要:** The webpage outlines the provisions for open work permits available to vulnerable migrant workers in Canada who are facing abuse or are at risk of it while on employer-specific work permits. Under section 207.1 of the Immigration and Refugee Protection Regulations, these workers can obtain an open work permit without needing a Labour Market Impact Assessment (LMIA), allowing them to leave their abusive employer and seek employment elsewhere. The policy aims to protect these individuals, facilitate their participation in investigations, and mitigate the risks associated with working irregularly due to abusive situations.

### 456. International Experience Canada (IEC) – [R204(d) - C21] – Reciprocity – International Mobility Program - Canada.ca

- **深度:** 10
- **链接数:** 86
- **摘要:** The International Experience Canada (IEC) program allows youth from participating countries to work in Canada, provided that Canadians have similar job opportunities abroad, thereby promoting reciprocal international relations. Participants are exempt from the Labour Market Impact Assessment (LMIA) and can engage in one of three categories: Working Holiday, Young Professionals, or International Co-op (Internship). The program aims to strengthen bilateral ties, facilitate applications from high-quality participants, and enhance international opportunities for young Canadians.

### 474. Entry/Exit Program - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/corporate/publications-manuals/operational-bulletins-manuals/service-delivery/entry-exit.html
- **重要性:** 0.80
- **深度:** 8
- **链接数:** 67
- **摘要:** The Entry/Exit Program is a collaborative initiative between Canada and the United States aimed at enhancing border security and efficiency by collecting and sharing travelers' biographic information, including entry and exit dates and modes of travel. Since the implementation of Bill C-21, data on all travelers—including Canadian and US citizens—has been gathered for land travel since July 2019, and for air travel since June 2020, with full compliance from air carriers expected by November 2022. The program facilitates access to this data for various government purposes, including immigration and investigations, while ensuring data protection and privacy.

### 537. Transit Without Visa Program: Find out if you’re eligible - Canada.ca

To qualify, travelers must possess a valid U.S. visa, a passport from specific countries (Indonesia, Philippines, Thailand, or Taiwan), and a confirmed onward ticket, among other conditions. Travelers must remain in the international transit area and depart Canada within 24 hours; otherwise, they may need to go through immigration.

### 540. Economic Mobility Pathways Pilot - Canada.ca

- **摘要:** The Economic Mobility Pathways Pilot (EMPP) is a Canadian immigration initiative designed to assist skilled refugees and displaced individuals in obtaining permanent residency through economic programs, thereby also providing Canadian employers with access to a new pool of qualified candidates. Eligible individuals can immigrate based on their work experience, education, and language skills, with or without a job offer.

### 541. Impact of immigration on Canada’s population growth 2014–2027 - Canada.ca

- **摘要:** The webpage discusses Canada's immigration projections and policies affecting population growth from 2014 to 2027, highlighting new targets for temporary residents beginning in 2025. It notes a significant decline in non-permanent residents, particularly international students, due to recent reforms aimed at capping admissions and limiting work permits. These measures are part of Canada's broader strategy to manage its immigration levels and achieve a net non-permanent resident population of 5% by the end of 2026.

Additionally, the Urgent Protection Program (UPP) addresses urgent cases of refugees at risk, including vulnerable women, ensuring they receive necessary assistance without the requirement to demonstrate settlement potential.

### 549. Interim Federal Health Program Policy - Canada.ca

- **摘要:** The Interim Federal Health Program (IFHP) in Canada offers limited and temporary health care coverage to vulnerable foreign nationals who do not qualify for provincial health insurance. It primarily serves resettled refugees, refugee claimants, protected persons, and other specific groups, providing essential health services within Canada as well as some pre-departure medical services for refugees selected for resettlement. However, not all migrants are eligible for this coverage, which is designed to address specific needs rather than serve all disadvantaged individuals.

### 552. Blended Visa Office-Referred Program: About the process - Canada.ca

- **摘要:** The Blended Visa Office-Referred (BVOR) Program allows Canadian citizens and permanent residents to sponsor refugees in need of resettlement, partnering with organizations like the UNHCR. This initiative not only helps refugees start anew in Canada but also enriches Canadian communities and fosters global humanitarian efforts.

### 569. Government-Assisted Refugees program - Canada.ca

### 594. Exemption from the employer compliance regime for the International Mobility Program - Canada.ca

- **摘要:** The webpage outlines the exemptions from the employer compliance regime under Canada's International Mobility Program (IMP) as established by amendments to the Immigration and Refugee Protection Regulations (IRPR) effective February 27, 2018. Certain employers, such as foreign missions, international organizations, and foreign governments, are not required to submit an offer of employment through the Employer Portal or pay the compliance fee when hiring foreign workers. However, foreign nationals must still provide necessary documentation to demonstrate their eligibility for a Labour Market Impact Assessment (LMIA) exemption when applying for a work permit.

Eligible travelers must arrive at a participating Canadian airport with a confirmed onward ticket and comply with travel document requirements. ### 607. Dual Canadian citizens need a valid Canadian passport - Canada.ca

- **摘要:** Dual Canadian citizens must have a valid Canadian passport to travel to or transit through Canada by air, as non-Canadian passports are no longer accepted for this purpose. For those without a Canadian passport at the time of travel, special authorization may be available, but generally, a valid Canadian passport is required to board flights to Canada.

### 621. Temporary Resident Permits (TRPs): Background and purpose - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/corporate/publications-manuals/operational-bulletins-manuals/temporary-residents/permits/background-purpose.html

- **深度:** 9
- **链接数:** 56
- **摘要:** Temporary Resident Permits (TRPs) in Canada allow inadmissible foreign nationals to enter or remain in the country under exceptional circumstances as authorized by designated officers. Introduced in 1910, TRPs provide temporary resident status, and if valid for at least six months, permit the holder to apply for work or study permits. The IRCC outlines the history and procedures surrounding TRPs to ensure transparency and accountability in their issuance.

Officers must adhere to specific criteria and document their recommendations thoroughly in compliance with IRPA and related regulations.

- **摘要:** The webpage outlines the procedures and requirements for health-care workers applying for permanent residence in Canada under temporary public policies related to COVID-19. Applications must be complete and labeled appropriately based on the applicant's intended province of residence, and they are submitted to the Humanitarian Migration Office in Vancouver. Incomplete applications will be returned, while complete submissions will receive an acknowledgment and be processed in the Global Case Management System.

### 697. Biometrics What we do after you give us your fingerprints and photo - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/services/biometrics/after-you-give.html
- **重要性:** 0.80
- **深度:** 9
- **链接数:** 67
- **摘要:** After you provide your biometrics (fingerprints and photo) for Canadian immigration, your information is encrypted and securely transmitted to a government database. During the application process, this data may be shared with the Royal Canadian Mounted Police and other law enforcement agencies for verification purposes. It's important to note that you have the right to refuse biometrics, but doing so may result in the refusal of your application.

### 698. Processing PRRA applications: General policy - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/corporate/publications-manuals/operational-bulletins-manuals/refugee-protection/removal-risk-assessment/applications-general-policy.html
- **重要性:** 0.80
- **深度:** 10
- **链接数:** 62
- **摘要:** The webpage provides an overview of the processing of Pre-Removal Risk Assessment (PRRA) applications in Canada, as outlined by the Immigration and Refugee Protection Act (IRPA). It details how PRRA ensures that Canada's immigration and refugee protection system aligns with international obligations and the Canadian Charter of Rights and Freedoms, and explains the grounds for considering PRRA applications, which are similar to those of the Immigration and Refugee Board (IRB). Most PRRA applications are reviewed through a paper process, but in certain exceptional cases, oral hearings may be conducted, ensuring a fair risk assessment for applicants.

### 701. Processing pre-removal risk assessment applications: Applicant restrictions on access to protection - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/corporate/publications-manuals/operational-bulletins-manuals/refugee-protection/removal-risk-assessment/applications-applicant-restrictions-on-access-protection.html
- **重要性:** 0.80
- **深度:** 10
- **链接数:** 71
- **摘要:** The webpage provides detailed guidelines from the IRCC regarding the processing of Pre-Removal Risk Assessment (PRRA) applications, specifically focusing on the restrictions for applicants described under subsection 112(3) of the Immigration and Refugee Protection Act (IRPA). These applicants, who may be inadmissible due to security concerns, serious criminality, or other specified grounds, are subject to limited access to protection and do not attain protected person status; instead, they receive a reviewable stay of removal. The document serves as a resource for stakeholders to understand the procedural framework surrounding these applications.

- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/corporate/publications-manuals/operational-bulletins-manuals/refugee-protection/removal-risk-assessment/non-refoulement.html

It explains that individuals who claim a risk of persecution in their country of origin can submit evidence within 30 days to support their case against removal. If submissions are made, a PRRA officer evaluates the risk, and the removals officer then decides whether the individual can be safely removed based on the assessment.

### 704. Processing in-Canada claims for protection: The Safe Third Country Agreement - Canada.ca

- **深度:** 10
- **链接数:** 87
- **摘要:** The webpage provides detailed information on the processing of in-Canada refugee claims in relation to the Safe Third Country Agreement (STCA) between Canada and the United States, which took effect on December 29, 2004. Under this agreement, individuals arriving in Canada from the US seeking refugee protection may be returned to the US unless they meet specific exceptions. The page outlines the conditions under which the STCA applies, the exemptions available, and the procedures for refugee claimants, making it a valuable resource for those interested in Canadian immigration and refugee protection policies.

### 715. Benefits of immigration on Canadian sectors - Canada.ca

- **摘要:** The webpage from Canada.ca outlines the significant contributions of immigrants to various sectors of the Canadian economy, highlighting that as of May 2021, they represented over 36% of workers in accommodation and food services, nearly 38% in transportation, and over 34% in professional services. The site emphasizes the ongoing need for immigrant talent in a growing economy, particularly in sectors facing labor shortages.

Workers must apply to extend or change their work permit if their employment conditions change or if they wish to continue working after their current permit expires.

- **摘要:** The Canada-Peru Free Trade Agreement (CPFTA) allows for the temporary entry of certain Peruvian business persons into Canada under the International Mobility Program, specifically under paragraph 204(a) of the Immigration and Refugee Protection Regulations. Signed in 2008 and effective from August 1, 2009, the CPFTA facilitates work permits for trade, service provision, and investment activities but does not assist with permanent residency or exempt applicants from standard requirements such as licensing or certification. ### 761. China Transit Program: Find out if you’re eligible - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/services/visit-canada/transit/without-visa/china-transit-eligibility.html
- **重要性:** 0.70
- **深度:** 9
- **链接数:** 60
- **摘要:** The China Transit Program (CTP) allows eligible Chinese travelers to transit through Canada without a visa when flying to or from the United States, provided they meet specific requirements. These include holding a valid U.S. visa, a valid passport from the People's Republic of China, and a confirmed airline ticket for a flight to the U.S. that departs within 24 hours of arrival in Canada. Travelers must also remain in the international transit area of designated Canadian airports and cannot leave the airport during their stopover. If they don't meet the eligibility criteria, they must apply for a transit visa.

### 768. Special program to sponsor Afghan refugees without refugee status from the UNHCR or a foreign state - Canada.ca

However, this program is now full, as all available spots have been filled. Those who have already applied will have their applications reviewed and processed, and they must keep their contact information updated throughout the sponsorship process.

### 812. Extending the validity of visas - Canada.ca

- **深度:** 10
- **链接数:** 54
- **摘要:** The webpage from Canada.ca outlines the policies and procedures regarding the extension of the validity of permanent resident visas (PRVs). It states that PRVs cannot be extended, and applicants who do not use their visa must reapply and pay a new processing fee, although they do not need to pay the right of permanent residence fee again. In exceptional cases where visas are issued with a validity of less than two months, applicants may have their visa updated and reissued if they cannot travel to Canada before expiration due to uncontrollable factors.

### 831. Canada-Colombia Free Trade Agreement (CCOFTA) overview – Agreements or arrangements – International Mobility Program - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/corporate/publications-manuals/operational-bulletins-manuals/temporary-residents/foreign-workers/international-free-trade-agreements/canada-colombia.html
- **重要性:** 0.60
- **深度:** 9
- **链接数:** 80
- **摘要:** The Canada-Colombia Free Trade Agreement (CCOFTA) allows for the temporary entry of certain business persons from Colombia to Canada under the International Mobility Program. Signed in 2008 and effective from 2011, the CCOFTA facilitates work permits for Colombian citizens engaged in trade, services, or investment activities, but does not provide a pathway for permanent residency or exempt individuals from standard requirements such as licensing or medical examinations. For more detailed policy and procedural guidance, the information is available on the IRCC website.

### 843. Medical surveillance - Canada.ca

Medical surveillance is necessary to monitor these individuals and ensure that any progression to active TB is addressed promptly, thereby protecting public health. The page outlines the process for medical surveillance, including the steps to take, how to maintain updated contact information, and what to expect during appointments.

### 852. Temporary public policy to facilitate issuance of permanent resident visas for certain foreign nationals outside Canada who are members of the families of Canadian victims of recent air disasters - Canada.ca

- **深度:** 9
- **链接数:** 54
- **摘要:** The Government of Canada has implemented a temporary public policy aimed at facilitating the issuance of permanent resident visas for certain foreign nationals outside Canada who are family members of Canadian victims from recent airline disasters. This policy, established in response to the Ethiopian Airlines flight 302 crash in 2019 and the downing of Ukraine International Airlines flight 752 in 2020, allows spouses, common-law partners, children, and some extended family members of the victims to apply for permanent residence in Canada. The initiative underscores the government's commitment to supporting the families affected by these tragic events.

### 875. Canada-Chile Free Trade Agreement (CCFTA) overview - Agreements or arrangements - International Mobility Program - Canada.ca

### 883. Operational Bulletin 348 - December 1, 2011 - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/corporate/publications-manuals/operational-bulletins-manuals/bulletins-2011/348-december-1-2011.html
- **重要性:** 0.50
- **深度:** 10
- **链接数:** 54
- **摘要:** Operational Bulletin 348, issued on December 1, 2011, by Citizenship and Immigration Canada, announces the elimination of counterfoils for approved permanent residence applicants from visa-exempt countries. Instead, these applicants will continue to receive a Confirmation of Permanent Residence (COPR) document, and officers will now have discretion regarding the necessity of seeing original passports versus photocopies. This change aims to streamline the process for applicants traveling from specific countries while maintaining essential record-keeping practices.

### 884. Public list of Employers who have been non-compliant - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/corporate/publications-manuals/operational-bulletins-manuals/temporary-residents/foreign-workers/eligibility/public-list-employers-who-have-been-non-compliant.html

- **深度:** 8
- **链接数:** 78
- **摘要:** The webpage from Canada.ca provides a public list of employers who have been found non-compliant with the regulations governing the International Mobility Program (IMP) managed by Immigration, Refugees and Citizenship Canada (IRCC). Employers may be listed if they receive an Administrative Monetary Penalty or a ban due to violations of compliance conditions. It's important to note that being on this list does not automatically render an employer ineligible to hire foreign nationals, as eligibility must be confirmed by IRCC processing officers.

### 890. Social Insurance Number – Overview - Canada.ca

- **重要性:** 0.40
- **深度:** 2
- **链接数:** 83
- **摘要:** The Social Insurance Number (SIN) is a crucial 9-digit identifier for individuals working in Canada or accessing government programs and benefits. Issued by Service Canada, the SIN must be protected as it is private and illegal for others to use. If you forget or lose your SIN, you can retrieve it through various means, including your My Service Canada Account, but note that the physical SIN card is no longer issued.

### 908. Temporary resident: Individuals named in an immigration warrant - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/corporate/publications-manuals/operational-bulletins-manuals/temporary-residents/visitors/individuals-named-immigration-warrant.html
- **重要性:** 0.40
- **深度:** 9
- **链接数:** 55
- **摘要:** The webpage from Canada.ca details the procedures and policies regarding individuals who are named in an immigration warrant issued by the Canada Border Services Agency (CBSA). It explains that if an inadmissible individual fails to comply with a request from a CBSA officer, a warrant may be issued for their arrest, which is then entered into the Canadian Police Information Centre (CPIC) system for law enforcement access. Additionally, it notes that when such an individual applies for immigration, the immigration authorities must inform the CBSA to ensure compliance with removal protocols.

### 909. Special processing measures: Persons directly affected by the 2024 wildfires throughout Canada - Canada.ca

Applications for these measures must be submitted by the November 30 deadline to be eligible.

### 922. Application process for airport authorities and air carriers: Transit Without Visa Program and China Transit Program - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/services/visit-canada/transit/without-visa/application-process.html
- **重要性:** 0.30
- **深度:** 10
- **链接数:** 58
- **摘要:** The webpage provides detailed information for airport authorities and air carriers interested in applying for Canada's Transit Without Visa (TWOV) Program and the China Transit Program (CTP). Applicants must complete specific application forms, submit two copies to both Immigration, Refugees and Citizenship Canada (IRCC) and the Canada Border Services Agency (CBSA), and sign a memorandum of understanding if approved. Proper completion of the forms is crucial to avoid delays in the assessment process.

### 923. Rural and Northern Immigration Pilot: who can apply - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/services/immigrate-canada/rural-northern-immigration-pilot/pr-eligibility.html
- **重要性:** 0.30
- **深度:** 8
- **链接数:** 81
- **摘要:** The Rural and Northern Immigration Pilot (RNIP) is a program that has ended accepting new applications as of August 31, 2024, but continues to process applications submitted before this date. To be eligible for RNIP, applicants must meet specific requirements, including having relevant work experience or education, meeting language and financial criteria, and intending to reside in the recommending community. Those eligible may still apply for a work permit while their application is being processed.

### 929. Check passport and travel document service standards - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/immigration-refugees-citizenship/services/canadian-passports/processing-times.html
- **重要性:** 0.30
- **深度:** 2
- **链接数:** 85
- **摘要:** The webpage provides information on the service standards for processing Canadian passport and travel document applications, outlining the typical wait times depending on the submission method. Regular passport applications submitted in person at a Service Canada Centre may take approximately 10 business days, while applications submitted by mail or online can take around 20 business days. For urgent requests, passports can be picked up by the end of the next business day or within 2 to 9 business days for express services; however, applicants are advised not to finalize travel plans until they receive their passport.

His dedication to developing culinary talent is evident through his long-standing role as an instructor and coach at Holland College's Culinary Institute of Canada.

Applicants can submit proof of work experience if they have recently acquired enough qualifying experience after applying.

- **摘要:** The webpage provides information about the Home Child Care Provider and Home Support Worker immigration pilots in Canada, specifically the Gaining Experience category for applying for permanent residence and an occupation-restricted open work permit from inside Canada. As of June 17, 2024, new applications are no longer accepted, but existing applications will continue to be processed. Recent changes now allow applicants to qualify with only 6 months of work experience, and eligible experience can be accumulated from both inside and outside Canada within a specified timeframe.

### 966. Immigration matters in sports - Canada.ca

The page emphasizes the integration of immigrants into Canadian sports culture, showcasing how they enhance the country's sporting achievements.

### 970. Parole Board of Canada - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/parole-board.html
- **重要性:** 0.10
- **深度:** 7
- **链接数:** 87
- **摘要:** The Parole Board of Canada (PBC) is an independent federal tribunal that plays a crucial role in the Canadian criminal justice system by making decisions regarding conditional releases of offenders, record suspensions, and clemency recommendations, all while prioritizing public safety. The PBC operates under the Corrections and Conditional Release Act and provides important services for victims of crime, including the right to be informed about offenders and to participate in the parole process. The PBC's decisions are made by Board Members who report to Parliament through the Minister of Public Safety.

### 979. Approach to HIV Screening - Canada.ca
- **URL:** https://www.canada.ca/en/public-health/services/publications/diseases-conditions/hiv-factsheet-types-screening-tests.html
- **重要性:** 0.10
- **深度:** 9
- **链接数:** 56
- **摘要:** The webpage from the Public Health Agency of Canada outlines the approach to HIV screening in Canada, detailing the types of tests available, including standard fourth-generation tests and rapid tests. Fourth-generation tests are preferred as they detect both HIV antibodies and the p24 antigen, providing earlier results, while rapid tests offer quick results but have longer window periods. It emphasizes the importance of confirmatory testing following a reactive result to ensure accurate diagnosis.

### 982. Guide 0128 – Pathway to permanent residence – In-Canada families of Canadian victims of recent air disasters - Canada.ca

- **链接数:** 120
- **摘要:** The webpage provides information about a now-closed public policy (Guide 0128) that facilitated pathways to permanent residence for families of Canadian victims of recent air disasters, specifically the Ethiopian Airlines crash in March 2019 and the downing of Ukraine International Airlines flight in January 2020. ### 996. Syphilis guide: Key information and resources - Canada.ca

- **摘要:** The Syphilis guide on Canada.ca provides essential information on the management of syphilis, including its risk factors, clinical manifestations, screening, diagnostic testing, treatment, and prevention. It highlights the significant public health concern posed by rising syphilis rates in Canada, particularly among gay, bisexual, and other men who have sex with men, as well as increasing cases among heterosexual populations and a resurgence of congenital syphilis.
